Resumo

Este trabalho tem por objetivo fazer a constru√ß√£o dos conjuntos num√©ricos dos inteiros,
racionais, reais e hiperreais. Para a constru√ß√£o dos n√∫meros inteiros e racionais foi utilizado o livro
‚ÄúN√∫meros Reais‚Äù de Jorge Aragona. No caso dos n√∫meros reais o livro ‚ÄúPrinciples of Mathematical
Analysis‚Äù de W. Rudin e, para a constru√ß√£o dos n√∫meros hiperreais o texto ‚ÄúAn Introduction to Non-
Standard Analysis‚Äù de I. Davis. Os textos foram utilizados para nortear esse trabalho, que tamb√©m
contempla os detalhes n√£o feitos pelos autores citados. A constru√ß√£o dos conjuntos num√©ricos, em
geral, apresenta caracter√≠sticas bem parecidas. A partir de um conjunto que serve como base, deÔ¨Åne-se
um elemento que posteriormente ser√° identiÔ¨Åcado com os elementos do conjunto a ser criado atrav√©s
de um isomorÔ¨Åsmo. As constru√ß√µes dos inteiros, racionais e hiperreais feitas aqui utilizam classes de
equival√™ncia, o que n√£o acontece na constru√ß√£o dos reais feita utilizando cortes de Dedekind, presente
nesta disserta√ß√£o. Al√©m dos cortes de Dedekind, existem outras maneiras de construir os n√∫meros
reais. Cantor, por exemplo, fez a constru√ß√£o utilizando sequ√™ncias de Cauchy, o que ser√° comentado
brevemente aqui. Al√©m das constru√ß√µes apontadas acima, o √∫ltimo cap√≠tulo desta disserta√ß√£o d√°
sugest√µes de como introduzir os t√≥picos estudados na matem√°tica do Ensino M√©dio, com exemplos
de atividades e trechos da hist√≥ria da matem√°tica que podem ser utilizados.

Palavras-chave: n√∫meros reais, n√∫meros hiperreais, constru√ß√£o de conjuntos num√©ricos.

Abstract

The goal of this work is to make the construction of the numerical sets of the integer,
rational, real and hyperreal numbers. For the construction of the integer and rational numbers it
was used the book ‚ÄúN√∫meros reais‚Äù by Jorge Aragona. In the case of the real numbers it was used
the book ‚ÄúPrinciples of Mathematical Analysis‚Äù by Walter Rudin and for the construction of the
hyperreal numbers it was used the text ‚ÄúAn introduction to the Non-Standard Analysis‚Äù by Isaac
Davis. These texts were used to guide this work, which also includes details not made by these
authors. The construction of numerical sets, in general, shows very similar characteristics. From a
set, which serves as a base to deÔ¨Åne an element that will be identiÔ¨Åed as elements in a new set, which
will be created through isomorphism. The constructions of integer, rational and hyperreal numbers
made here use equivalence classes, which does not happen in the construction of the real numbers
that were made using the Dedekind cuts, in this dissertation. In addition to Dedekind cuts, there are
other ways to construct real numbers. Cantor, for instance, made the construction of real numbers
using Cauchy sequences, which are going to be commented brieÔ¨Çy here. Besides the construction
mentioned above, the last chapter gives suggestions about how to introduce studied topics in the high
school mathematics level, exemplifying activities and passages about mathematics history that can be
used.

Keywords: real numbers, hyperreal numbers, construction of the numerical sets.
